in the system which are * directly or indirectly relevant to compiling Whiley files. For example, * source folders containing whiley files are (obviously) directly relevant; * however, other containers may be relevant (e.g. if they hold jar files on the * whileypath). * </p> * * <p> * When a resource changes which is relevant to the builder (e.g. a Whiley file, * etc) then the WhileyProject must be notified of this. In turn, it updates its * knowledge of the system accordingly and may schedule files to be rebuilt. * </p> * * @author David J. Pearce */<CODESPLIT> p  a whileyproject responsible managing resources system directly indirectly relevant compiling whiley files example  source folders whiley files  obviously  directly relevant  however  containers relevant  eg hold jar files whileypath    p   p  a resource relevant builder  eg a whiley file  etc  whileyproject notified this turn  updates knowledge system schedule files rebuilt   p   author david j pearce<CODESPLIT>externalRoots; binaryRoots; sourceRoots; delta; builder; rules; registry = new Content.Registry() {    public void associate(Path.Entry e) {        if (e.suffix().equals("whiley")) {            e.associate(WhileyFile.ContentType, null);        } else if (e.suffix().equals("class")) {            // this could be either a normal JVM class, or a Wyil class. We            // need to determine which.            try {                WyilFile c = WyilFile.ContentType.read(e, e.inputStream());                if (c != null) {                    e.associate(WyilFile.ContentType, c);                }            } catch (Exception ex) {            // hmmm, not ideal            }        }    }    public String suffix(Content.Type<?> t) {        if (t == WhileyFile.ContentType) {            return "whiley";        } else if (t == WyilFile.ContentType) {            return "class";        } else {            return "dat";        }    }}; <CODESPLIT> vazio externalroots  binaryroots  sourceroots  delta  builder  rules registry  elseif e suffix   equals  class      thiscouldbeeitheranormaljvmclass orawyilclass we  needtodeterminewhich try wyilfilec if c    catch exceptionex    hmmm notideal   publicstringsuffix content type   t  if t  elseif t           else              return  dat                    <CODESPLIT> vazio externalroots  binaryroots  sourceroots  delta  builder  rules registry  elseif suffix   equals  class      thiscouldbeeitheranormaljvmclass orawyilclass  needtodeterminewhich wyilfilec    catch exceptionex    hmmm notideal   publicstringsuffix content type     elseif                        return  dat<CODESPLIT><VAZIO>[ initialise ][ setLogger ][ exists ][ get ][ get ][ match ][ flush ][ refresh ][ changed ][ added ][ removed ][ clean ][ build ][ buildAll ][ highlightSyntaxError ]<CODESPLIT><vazio>[ initialise ][ set logger ][ exists ][ get ][ get ][ match ][ flush ][ refresh ][ changed ][ added ][ removed ][ clean ][ build ][ build all ][ highlight syntax error ] <CODESPLIT><vazio>[ initialise set logger exists match flush refresh changed added removed clean build build highlight syntax error <CODESPLIT>[<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [<VAZIO>] [/** * A resource of some sort has changed, and we need to update the namespace * accordingly.
